I come here for a quick pizza fix and when Im on a budget. The new $6 pizza is extra cheesy and tastes better than the regular $5 one. This place is convenient because they let you order online, and you can pick up your order quickly. This is good if you need to order a lot of boxes. This pizza is good to eat at the moment, but it doesnt taste good when reheated. Overall, this is a good place to come get quick pizza for a good price.<//Review>

$8.73
Average Little Caesars hourly pay ranges from approximately $8.73 per hour for Supervisor to $12.73 per hour for Junior Managing Director.

Little Caesars pays $8.73 an hour. Last time I visit little ceasers I seen about 4 employees working inside the restaurant.

Let's do the math. $8.73 x 8 hours = $69.84 Little Caesars pays their employees a day.

I'm estimating little ceasers sells approximately 10 pizzas in one hour. $7 a pizza.

$7 x 10 in hour = $70

Little Caesars makes $70 in one hour of sells. They are open 8 hours a day.

$70 x 8 = $560

Little ceasers makes approximately $560 in 8 hours a day. And pays their employees $69.84 a day.

Little Ceasers makes $560 in 8 hours and pays their employees - $279.36 out of the $560 a day they make in sells.

$560 - $279.36 = $280.64

Little Ceasers makes $280.64 a day approximately in profits. Whit pay employees.

In one week little ceasers makes $1,403.02

In one month little ceasers makes
$5,612.80 of profits.

$67,353.60  a year of profits. Little ceasers been in business for about 5 years now approximately:  $336,738.00 in five years little ceasers makes profits selling pizzas at $7.

There's a reason why they still in business.< /text>

< Review>
I used BHTS services to move from LA, California to Cleveland, Ohio.
I sent them a request over their website, next day they called me and arranged an appointment. 2 employee came morning (Arianne and Mike), on time as scheduled, they called 30 minutes prior to coming. They evaluated my stuff, they were very professional and friendly. I felt comfortable to deal and communicate with them.
They explained their system, how many days it gonna take, the assembling, unloading, brief history about the company and little statistics.
At night I received an email from them with the estimate price, weight and all the details.
I did 90% of packing by myself. they did the refrigerator, beds, mattresses, Guitar and they did extra warping to my "warped" tables.
They got a parking permit, 5 days prior to the move there was signs on the street side. the guy who came to do the evaluation kept communicating with me via e-mail and he answered all my question fast! as soon as he got it! days, night even weekends. Which was super great!!

On the moving day May 10th, the driver called me 30 minutes prior to the appointment, he came on time with his helpers, they put a "Red Carpet" which was cool (Hollywood style ;) ). the driver was friendly and immediately started to put stickers on all the boxes with a serial number, one by one. He was professional with what he was doing. then they started to take the boxes to the truck.
within 5 hours they were done. the helpers were very friendly and cooperative. they handled my stuff with care.
He gave me my copies of the inventory and he gave me his phone number to truck him. he told me when to expect my stuff to arrive in Ohio!
I had some worries as I saw some boxes I marked as "Fragile" on the base line in the truck! I communicated the BHTS guys on spot, and they replied on spot as well! they checked with the driver and assured me and explained to me their packing and loading technique.

On May 22nd I received a phone call from the driver telling me that he is coming next day morning. May 23rd the same driver called me that he arrived, he examined the alley, however, it was narrow for the truck, so he explained that he will need an hour to rent  a smaller truck. after an hour, a smaller truck brought my stuff with the driver and 2 helpers. within 3 hours all my stuff were in my new apartment. The helpers tried to put each box in the correct room but they didn't do great with that! one of the helper was friendly, yet the other wasn't at all!!.
They assembled the refrigerator for me, as they had to take the doors off in California (it was huge compering to the apartments door).

Nothing was broken, nothing was scratched, nothing was missing.
Well, I found 1 tiny dish broken!! but it was 7700 Ib shipment and all was in the same condition as I gave, except that tiny dish, so it is FINE.

Over all the experience was great, If I moved again, I'm gonna use their services too and for sure I recommend it for you. :)

Professional, Friendly, Punctual and they answer any question, as soon as possible :)
I'm satisfied.
BHTS God Bless you, I give you 5 star ^_^</Review>

Popular sandwich shop that I'm not sure if it lives up to the hype. The wait was about 10 minute around noon and I had a Smoking Joe sandwich which was wrapped nice and warm. The portion is definitely decent, especially when you feel it in your hand.

I really want to like this place, I really do. It is a short 5 minutes walk from me instead of 5 mins drive to Cafe Leche. But the coffee is just too inconsistent. I have tried Charlie's about 4 times in the last 3 years. Each time I said no more but the desire to support local business implore me to give it one more try.

Today's coffee is Guatemalan, my favorite beans in the world. It was weak and tasted bland.

Oh well, back to my 5 minutes drive.<//Review>

< review>
Definitely a "good neighbor"

We've been with State Farm for over a couple of decades, primarily because of Steven Wang, and his friendly Staff.

From the moment we signed up for auto insurance, we've added many various lines over the years during our personal review of our situation along the timeline of this thing called life. Not only in the good times when we are on solid ground (knock on wood, as we're in Southern California!) but even when we've had a major claim on our home. We definitely appreciate the answers to our many questions during these moments and appreciate the human aspect Steven and his Staff exhibit towards my family.

We continue hitting new milestones and recently a major one happened: adding a teen driver to our policy (Yay! ...we now have a personal Uber driver!). Kimberly and Bima walked us through our options so we could choose the best route, while at the same time cross-checking our coverages to make sure the current situation matched our expectations for coverages. Just in this short duration of friendly conversation, we were able to discover yet another discount that we now qualified for (thanks, Kimberly and Bima, for taking the time to chat outside of the "just insure our son" scenario).

We've always felt welcome in working with Steven and his Staff, and we look forward to future conversations in many years to come!

I encourage those looking for an office of insurance professionals to seriously consider speaking with Steven and his Staff, and just get to know them!</review>

<Name>Bryan Tsunoda<//Name>< Date>
1393132249533<//Date>
<Rate>4< /Rate><Text>Trader Joe's is a specialty grocer that offers quality food for very reasonable prices. This location is particularly challenging because it is smaller than the average Trader Joe's and the parking lot is almost aways full.

Just entering Trader Joe's is sometimes challenging. People are usually in a hurry and want to exit and I've often had to wait for a stream of people to go by before it's "safe" to enter.

The produce section is ok. Many items are in stryofoam trays wrapped in plastic wrap. I guess until they install scales the register, this will always be the case. Much of the produce is shipped from Mexico, Chile or New Zealand and so if you're looking for local produce, you probably won't find it here.

The freezer case is well stocked. They offer frozen prepared entrees and side dishes. Vegetables, meats, fish and desserts are also available in the two frozen cases.

This location has a pretty good selection of cheese. If you're looking to purchase appetizers for a party, this is a good place to come for that. Even the frozen case and some interesting items that make good 'last minute" hot appetizers.

The wine selection is average for a Trader Joe's and I wonder why they devote so much floor space for two buck Chuck (Charles Shaw).

Rush hour is in the late afternoons to early evenings. The best time to come to this location is when they open (either on the weekday or weekend).  Don't even think of coming here the evening before a major holiday like July 4 or Memorial Day.<//Text>< pictures>
None< /pictures>
